## §2.1 `M01-A` — Reverential Fear / Fear of God

_The fear of the Lord as the proper inner orientation — reverential awe before divine majesty, the beginning of wisdom, the ground of covenant obedience and worship. God is the object; wisdom, holiness, and faithful conduct are the outcomes._

1. Terms in sub-group (19): G5156 tromos, G5399 fobeō, G5401 fobos, G6015 deos, H1481C gur, H2730 cha.red, H2865 cha.tat, H3372G ya.re, H3372H ya.re, H3373 ya.re, H3374 yir.ah, H4035 me.gu.rah, H4172A mo.rah, H4172B mo.ra, H6206 a.rats, H6342 pa.chad, H6343 pa.chad, H6345 pach.dah, H7578 re.tet
2. Verse-context groups in sub-group (44):

## §2.2 `M01-B` — Threatening / Creaturely Fear

_The alarm-response to perceived danger — fear of enemies, threatening powers, circumstances, and death. Includes the divine 'do not fear' reassurance commands, whose meaning requires the threatening fear to be identified._

1. Terms in sub-group (13): G1630 ekfobos, G1719 emfobos, G4422 ptoeō, G4423 ptoēsis, G4426 pturomai, G5398 foberos, H1763 de.chal, H2119B za.chal, H3016 ya.gor, H3025 ya.gor, H4032 ma.gor, H4034 me.go.rah, H7297 ra.hah
2. Verse-context groups in sub-group (15):

### §2.2.1 Group `1690-001` (id=248) — G4422 ptoeō

_Inner state of terror or startled fright — inner person overwhelmed and destabilised by sudden or threatening encounters_

**Anchor verse:**

| Reference | Term | Verse text | Observation |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Luk 21:9** | G4422 ptoeō | Luk 21:9 And when you hear of wars and tumults , do not be terrified , for these things must first take place , but the end will not be at once .” |  |

|---|---|---|---|

---

## §2.3 `M01-C` — Terror and Dread

_Overwhelming, acute terror — externally imposed, comprehensive, often divinely sent. The inner being not merely afraid but engulfed, overwhelmed, and shattered. The most intense end of the fear spectrum._

1. Terms in sub-group (17): H0366 a.yom, H0367 e.mah, H1091 bal.la.hah, H1205 be.a.tah, H2189 za.a.vah, H2283 chag.ga, H2844A chat, H2847 chit.tah, H2849 chat.chat, H2851 chit.tit, H2866 cha.tat, H4288 me.chit.tah, H4637 ma.a.ra.tsah, H4712 me.tsar, H6178 a.ruts, H8047G sham.mah, H8606 tiph.le.tset
2. Verse-context groups in sub-group (15):

### §2.3.1 Group `162-001` (id=79) — H4712 me.tsar

|---|---|---|---|

## §2.4 `M01-D` — Dismay and Alarm

_The destabilising, paralysing form of fear — the inner collapse of composure under threat; the overwhelmed and immobilised inner person, unable to act._

1. Terms in sub-group (5): H0926 ba.hal, H0927 be.hal, H2865 cha.tat, H3735 ke.ra, H8541 tim.ma.hon
2. Verse-context groups in sub-group (9):

### §2.4.1 Group `703-001` (id=250) — H2865 cha.tat

## §2.5 `M01-E` — Trembling and Shuddering

_The somatic-inner expression of fear, dread, and awe — trembling and shuddering as the felt inner-bodily manifestation across the full fear spectrum. Names what fear looks like as it moves through the body-inner interface._

1. Terms in sub-group (19): G1790 entromos, G5156 tromos, H2113 ze.va.ah, H2729 cha.rad, H2730 cha.red, H2731 cha.ra.dah, H6206 a.rats, H6426 pa.lats, H6427 pal.la.tsut, H7264 ra.gaz, H7268 rag.gaz, H7269 rog.zah, H7374 re.tet, H7460 ra.ad, H7461A ra.ad, H7461B re.a.dah, H8175A sa.ar, H8178A sa.ar, H8429 te.vah
2. Verse-context groups in sub-group (27):

### §2.5.1 Group `1554-001` (id=147) — H7264 ra.gaz

_Term names the trembling restraint of anger — being agitated without sin, holding inner fury still before God in the privacy of the heart_

**Verses:** 3 connected (1 anchor, 2 other)  

**Anchor verse:**

| Reference | Term | Verse text | Observation |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Psa 4:4** | H7264 ra.gaz | Psa 4:4 Be angry , and do not sin ; ponder in your own hearts on your beds , and be silent . Selah |  |

**Other verses related to the context:**

| Reference | Term | Verse text | Observation |
|---|---|---|---|
| Psa 77:16 | H7264 ra.gaz | Psa 77:16 When the waters saw you, O God , when the waters saw you, they were afraid ; indeed , the deep trembled . |  |
| Psa 99:1 | H7264 ra.gaz | Psa 99:1 The Lord reigns ; let the peoples tremble ! He sits enthroned upon the cherubim ; let the earth quake ! |  |

## §2.6 `M01-F` — Anxiety

_Chronic, anticipatory inner-being agitation — accumulated apprehensive thoughts, worried restlessness, the inner person dwelling on feared possibilities. Temporal structure is forward-looking and sustained, not immediate-response._

1. Terms in sub-group (3): G0085 ademoneo, H1674 de.a.gah, H8312 sar.ap.pim
2. Verse-context groups in sub-group (4):

## §2.7 `M01-G` — Awe and Wonder

_Overwhelmed astonishment before the extraordinary — the wonder-fear response to divine action, miraculous presence, or the unexpected. Astonishment is the primary element; fear is secondary and derivative._

1. Terms in sub-group (4): G1568 ekthambeo, G1569 ekthambos, G2285 thambos, H8539 ta.mah
2. Verse-context groups in sub-group (4):

### §2.7.3 Group `289-001` (id=1053) — H8539 ta.mah

## §2.8 `M01-H` — Timidity and Cowardice

_The dispositional form of fear — the settled inner orientation of fearfulness that impairs faith and action. Cowardice as a moral inner condition: the person characterised by chronic fearfulness rather than trust._

1. Terms in sub-group (3): G1167 deilia, G1168 deiliaō, G1169 deilos
2. Verse-context groups in sub-group (4):

### §2.8.1 Group `261-001` (id=891) — G1168 deiliaō

_Term names the inner condition of fearful disturbance — the troubled, afraid state of heart that Christ's peace displaces_

**Verses:** 1 connected (1 anchor, 0 other)  

**Anchor verse:**

| Reference | Term | Verse text | Observation |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Joh 14:27** | G1168 deiliaō | Joh 14:27 Peace I leave with you ; my peace I give to you . Not as the world gives do I give to you . Let not your hearts be troubled , neither let them be afraid . |  |

### §2.8.2 Group `288-001` (id=918) — G1167 deilia

| Reference | Term | Verse text | Observation |
|---|---|---|---|
